With <s>upa, ni, vi</s> or <s>sam</s> the verb is deponent (<s>upahnayate</s>); also with <s>AG</s> if rivalry be signified, (<s>Ahvayate</s>) he challenges.</body><tail><L>98209</L><pc>982</pc></tail></H1>
